<script type="text/x-dc" data-dc-script>
class Component extends DCLogic {
  state = { nav: 'agenda', calView: 'month', selMonth: 5, selDay: 11 };

  // ---- icons ----
  ic(name, size, color) {
    const R = React.createElement;
    const S = (kids) => R('svg', { width: size, height: size, viewBox: '0 0 24 24', fill: 'none', stroke: color, strokeWidth: 2, strokeLinecap: 'round', strokeLinejoin: 'round', style: { display: 'block', flex: '0 0 auto' } }, kids);
    const p = (d, i) => R('path', { key: 'p' + i, d });
    const c = (cx, cy, r, i) => R('circle', { key: 'c' + i, cx, cy, r });
    const cal = R('rect', { key: 'rect', x: 3, y: 4, width: 18, height: 18, rx: 2 });
    switch (name) {
      case 'menu': return S([p('M4 6h16', 0), p('M4 12h16', 1), p('M4 18h16', 2)]);
      case 'plus': return S([p('M5 12h14', 0), p('M12 5v14', 1)]);
      case 'x': return S([p('M18 6 6 18', 0), p('M6 6l12 12', 1)]);
      case 'left': return S([p('m15 18-6-6 6-6', 0)]);
      case 'right': return S([p('m9 18 6-6-6-6', 0)]);
      case 'scissors': return S([c(6, 6, 3, 0), c(6, 18, 3, 1), p('M20 4 8.12 15.88', 2), p('M14.47 14.48 20 20', 3), p('M8.12 8.12 12 12', 4)]);
      case 'arrow': return S([c(12, 12, 10, 0), p('M12 8l4 4-4 4', 1), p('M8 12h8', 2)]);
      case 'calendar-check': return S([cal, p('M16 2v4', 1), p('M8 2v4', 2), p('M3 10h18', 3), p('m9 16 2 2 4-4', 4)]);
      case 'calendar-days': return S([cal, p('M16 2v4', 1), p('M8 2v4', 2), p('M3 10h18', 3), p('M8 14h.01', 4), p('M12 14h.01', 5), p('M16 14h.01', 6), p('M8 18h.01', 7), p('M12 18h.01', 8), p('M16 18h.01', 9)]);
      case 'list': return S([p('M8 6h13', 0), p('M8 12h13', 1), p('M8 18h13', 2), p('M3 6h.01', 3), p('M3 12h.01', 4), p('M3 18h.01', 5)]);
      case 'wallet': return S([p('M21 12V7H5a2 2 0 0 1 0-4h14v4', 0), p('M3 5v14a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h16v-5', 1), p('M18 12a2 2 0 0 0 0 4h4v-4Z', 2)]);
      default: return S([]);
    }
  }

  // ---- data ----
  get appts() {
    return [
      { day: 10, start: '15:00', dur: 40, client: 'Marcos', service: 'Corte' },
      { day: 11, start: '10:00', dur: 90, client: 'Sofía', service: 'Coloración' },
      { day: 11, start: '12:00', dur: 45, client: 'Diego', service: 'Corte' },
      { day: 11, start: '14:30', dur: 90, client: 'Camila', service: 'Coloración' },
      { day: 12, start: '09:30', dur: 90, client: 'Juancitopipon', service: 'Coloración' },
      { day: 12, start: '14:30', dur: 90, client: 'Juancito', service: 'Coloración' },
      { day: 13, start: '12:30', dur: 90, client: 'Asa', service: 'Coloración' },
      { day: 17, start: '11:00', dur: 45, client: 'Bruno', service: 'Corte' },
      { day: 20, start: '16:00', dur: 60, client: 'Leo', service: 'Tratamiento' },
    ];
  }
  svc(name) {
    const m = {
      'Coloración': { c: '#7FA9FF', bg: '#141E33', bd: '#2A3A5E' },
      'Corte': { c: '#34D399', bg: '#10231B', bd: '#1E4636' },
      'Peinado': { c: '#E8A33D', bg: '#241B0E', bd: '#4A3A1C' },
      'Tratamiento': { c: '#B79CFF', bg: '#1E1830', bd: '#392E5E' },
    };
    return m[name] || m['Corte'];
  }
  apptsForDay(mo, d) { return mo === 5 ? this.appts.filter(a => a.day === d) : []; }

  // ---- date helpers ----
  monthsFull() { return ['Enero', 'Febrero', 'Marzo', 'Abril', 'Mayo', 'Junio', 'Julio', 'Agosto', 'Septiembre', 'Octubre', 'Noviembre', 'Diciembre']; }
  monthsAbbr() { return ['Ene', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Abr', 'May', 'Jun', 'Jul', 'Ago', 'Sep', 'Oct', 'Nov', 'Dic']; }
  daysInMonth(y, m) { return new Date(y, m + 1, 0).getDate(); }
  firstWdMon(y, m) { return (new Date(y, m, 1).getDay() + 6) % 7; } // 0 = Monday
  monthCells(y, m) {
    const lead = this.firstWdMon(y, m), n = this.daysInMonth(y, m), cells = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < lead; i++) cells.push(null);
    for (let d = 1; d <= n; d++) cells.push(d);
    while (cells.length % 7 !== 0) cells.push(null);
    return cells;
  }
  isToday(m, d) { return m === 5 && d === 11; }
  parseMin(t) { const [h, mi] = t.split(':').map(Number); return h * 60 + mi; }

  // ---- bottom nav ----
  buildNav() {
    const R = React.createElement;
    const items = [
      { key: 'hoy', label: 'Hoy', icon: 'calendar-check' },
      { key: 'turnos', label: 'Turnos', icon: 'list' },
      { key: 'agenda', label: 'Agenda', icon: 'calendar-days' },
      { key: 'ganancias', label: 'Ganancias', icon: 'wallet' },
    ];
    const active = this.state.nav;
    return R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', borderTop: '1px solid #232325', background: '#161617', padding: '10px 6px 18px', flex: '0 0 auto' } },
      items.map(it => {
        const on = it.key === active, col = on ? '#2F6BFF' : '#6F6F73';
        return R('button', {
          key: it.key,
          onClick: () => {
            if (it.key === 'agenda') this.setState({ nav: 'agenda', calView: 'month' });
            else if (it.key === 'hoy') this.setState({ nav: 'hoy', selMonth: 5, selDay: 11 });
            else this.setState({ nav: it.key });
          },
          style: { flex: 1, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', gap: '4px', background: 'transparent', border: 0, cursor: 'pointer', padding: '4px 0', color: col, transition: 'color .15s' }
        }, this.ic(it.icon, 21, col), R('span', { style: { fontSize: '10px', fontWeight: on ? 700 : 600 } }, it.label));
      }));
  }

  // ---- appbar (shared) ----
  appbar() {
    const R = React.createElement;
    return R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '11px', padding: '6px 18px 12px', flex: '0 0 auto' } },
      R('span', { style: { cursor: 'pointer', display: 'flex' } }, this.ic('menu', 22, '#ADADB0')),
      R('span', { style: { width: '28px', height: '28px', borderRadius: '8px', background: '#1C1C1E', border: '1px solid #38383B', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' } }, this.ic('scissors', 15, '#2F6BFF')),
      R('span', { style: { fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '16px', flex: 1 } }, 'BarberFras'),
      R('span', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '5px', background: '#2F6BFF', color: '#fff', fontSize: '12px', fontWeight: 700, padding: '7px 11px', borderRadius: '10px', cursor: 'pointer' } }, this.ic('plus', 15, '#fff'), 'Turno')
    );
  }

  // ---- YEAR ----
  yearView() {
    const R = React.createElement, y = 2026;
    const mini = (m) => {
      const cells = this.monthCells(y, m);
      return R('button', {
        key: m, onClick: () => this.setState({ calView: 'month', selMonth: m }),
        style: { background: 'transparent', border: 0, padding: '4px', cursor: 'pointer', textAlign: 'left' }
      },
        R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '15px', color: m === 5 ? '#2F6BFF' : '#F4F4F2', marginBottom: '5px' } }, this.monthsAbbr()[m]),
        R('div', { style: { display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(7,1fr)', gap: '1px' } },
          cells.map((d, i) => R('div', {
            key: i,
            style: {
              fontSize: '8px', textAlign: 'center', lineHeight: '11px', height: '11px',
              fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace",
              color: !d ? 'transparent' : (this.isToday(m, d) ? '#fff' : '#8A8A8E'),
              background: d && this.isToday(m, d) ? '#2F6BFF' : 'transparent',
              borderRadius: '50%', fontWeight: d && this.isToday(m, d) ? 700 : 400
            }
          }, d || '·')))
      );
    };
    return R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', height: '100%' } },
      this.appbar(),
      R('div', { style: { padding: '2px 18px 10px', flex: '0 0 auto' } },
        R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '30px' } }, '2026')),
      R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, overflowY: 'auto', padding: '0 14px 16px', display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(3,1fr)', gap: '10px', alignContent: 'start' } },
        this.monthsAbbr().map((_, m) => mini(m)))
    );
  }

  // ---- MONTH ----
  monthView() {
    const R = React.createElement, y = 2026, m = this.state.selMonth;
    const cells = this.monthCells(y, m);
    const wd = ['L', 'M', 'M', 'J', 'V', 'S', 'D'];
    const dayCell = (d, i) => {
      if (!d) return R('div', { key: i, style: { height: '46px' } });
      const aps = this.apptsForDay(m, d), today = this.isToday(m, d);
      return R('button', {
        key: i, onClick: () => this.setState({ calView: 'day', selDay: d }),
        style: { height: '46px', background: 'transparent', border: 0, cursor: 'pointer', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', gap: '3px', padding: '4px 0' }
      },
        R('span', { style: { width: '24px', height: '24px', borderRadius: '50%', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', fontSize: '13px', fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontWeight: today ? 700 : 500, color: today ? '#fff' : '#E4E4E6', background: today ? '#2F6BFF' : 'transparent' } }, d),
        R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', gap: '2px', height: '5px' } },
          aps.slice(0, 3).map((a, k) => R('span', { key: k, style: { width: '5px', height: '5px', borderRadius: '50%', background: this.svc(a.service).c } })))
      );
    };
    return R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', height: '100%' } },
      this.appbar(),
      R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', padding: '0 18px 10px', flex: '0 0 auto' } },
        R('button', { onClick: () => this.setState({ calView: 'year' }), style: { background: 'transparent', border: 0, cursor: 'pointer', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'baseline', gap: '7px', padding: 0 } },
          R('span', { style: { fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '26px', color: '#fff' } }, this.monthsFull()[m]),
          R('span', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontSize: '13px', color: '#6F6F73' } }, '2026')),
        R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', gap: '4px' } },
          R('span', { onClick: () => this.setState({ selMonth: (m + 11) % 12 }), style: { width: '32px', height: '32px', borderRadius: '9px', background: '#1C1C1E', border: '1px solid #2A2A2C', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', cursor: 'pointer' } }, this.ic('left', 16, '#ADADB0')),
          R('span', { onClick: () => this.setState({ selMonth: (m + 1) % 12 }), style: { width: '32px', height: '32px', borderRadius: '9px', background: '#1C1C1E', border: '1px solid #2A2A2C', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', cursor: 'pointer' } }, this.ic('right', 16, '#ADADB0')))
      ),
      R('div', { style: { display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(7,1fr)', padding: '0 14px 6px', flex: '0 0 auto' } },
        wd.map((w, i) => R('div', { key: i, style: { textAlign: 'center', fontSize: '10px', fontWeight: 700, letterSpacing: '.08em', color: '#6F6F73' } }, w))),
      R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, overflowY: 'auto', padding: '0 14px 14px' } },
        R('div', { style: { display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(7,1fr)' } }, cells.map((d, i) => dayCell(d, i))))
    );
  }

  // ---- DAY ----
  dayView() {
    const R = React.createElement, y = 2026, m = this.state.selMonth, d = this.state.selDay, hoy = this.state.nav === 'hoy';
    const aps = this.apptsForDay(m, d);
    // week strip (Mon..Sun containing d)
    const wdMon = (new Date(y, m, d).getDay() + 6) % 7;
    const monday = d - wdMon;
    const dim = this.daysInMonth(y, m);
    const wdLabels = ['L', 'M', 'M', 'J', 'V', 'S', 'D'];
    const strip = R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', gap: '4px', padding: '4px 14px 12px', flex: '0 0 auto' } },
      [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6].map(i => {
        const dd = monday + i, valid = dd >= 1 && dd <= dim, sel = dd === d, t = this.isToday(m, dd);
        const has = valid && this.apptsForDay(m, dd).length > 0;
        return R('button', {
          key: i, onClick: () => valid && this.setState({ nav: 'agenda', calView: 'day', selDay: dd }),
          style: { flex: 1, background: sel ? '#16203A' : 'transparent', border: sel ? '1px solid #2A3A5E' : '1px solid transparent', borderRadius: '12px', padding: '7px 0', cursor: valid ? 'pointer' : 'default', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', gap: '3px' }
        },
          R('span', { style: { fontSize: '10px', fontWeight: 700, color: sel ? '#7FA9FF' : '#6F6F73' } }, wdLabels[i]),
          R('span', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontSize: '15px', fontWeight: sel ? 700 : 500, color: !valid ? '#3A3A3D' : (t ? '#2F6BFF' : (sel ? '#fff' : '#D9D9DB')) } }, valid ? dd : ''),
          R('span', { style: { width: '5px', height: '5px', borderRadius: '50%', background: has ? '#7FA9FF' : 'transparent' } }));
      }));

    // timeline
    const startH = 9, endH = 20, hourPx = 52;
    const hours = [];
    for (let h = startH; h <= endH; h++) {
      hours.push(R('div', { key: 'h' + h, style: { position: 'absolute', top: (h - startH) * hourPx + 'px', left: 0, right: 0, height: hourPx + 'px' } },
        R('span', { style: { position: 'absolute', left: 0, top: '-7px', width: '44px', fontSize: '11px', fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", color: '#5A5A5E', textAlign: 'right' } }, ('0' + h).slice(-2) + ':00'),
        R('span', { style: { position: 'absolute', left: '52px', right: '8px', top: 0, height: '1px', background: '#1E1E20' } })));
    }
    const blocks = aps.map((a, k) => {
      const s = this.svc(a.service), top = (this.parseMin(a.start) - startH * 60) / 60 * hourPx, ht = a.dur / 60 * hourPx;
      return R('div', {
        key: 'b' + k,
        style: { position: 'absolute', left: '56px', right: '10px', top: top + 'px', height: (ht - 4) + 'px', background: s.bg, borderLeft: '3px solid ' + s.c, borderRadius: '9px', padding: '6px 10px', overflow: 'hidden' }
      },
        R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontSize: '10px', color: s.c, fontWeight: 700 } }, a.start),
        R('div', { style: { fontSize: '13px', fontWeight: 700, color: '#F4F4F2', whiteSpace: 'nowrap', overflow: 'hidden', textOverflow: 'ellipsis' } }, a.client),
        ht > 38 ? R('div', { style: { fontSize: '11px', color: '#ADADB0' } }, a.service) : null);
    });
    const emptyMsg = aps.length === 0 ? R('div', { style: { position: 'absolute', top: '120px', left: '56px', right: '10px', textAlign: 'center', color: '#5A5A5E', fontSize: '13px' } }, 'Sin turnos este día — libre 🎉') : null;

    const header = R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', padding: '0 18px 8px', flex: '0 0 auto' } },
      R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '10px' } },
        hoy ? null : R('button', { onClick: () => this.setState({ calView: 'month' }), style: { width: '32px', height: '32px', borderRadius: '9px', background: '#1C1C1E', border: '1px solid #2A2A2C', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', cursor: 'pointer' } }, this.ic('left', 16, '#ADADB0')),
        R('div', null,
          R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '24px', color: '#fff', lineHeight: 1.05 } }, (hoy ? 'Hoy · ' : '') + d + ' ' + this.monthsAbbr()[m]),
          R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', color: '#6F6F73' } }, aps.length + ' turno' + (aps.length === 1 ? '' : 's') + ' · ' + (aps.length ? Math.round(aps.length / 12 * 100) + '% ocupación' : 'día libre')))));

    return R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', height: '100%' } },
      this.appbar(),
      header,
      strip,
      R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, overflowY: 'auto', padding: '6px 14px 20px' } },
        R('div', { style: { position: 'relative', height: (endH - startH) * hourPx + 'px' } }, hours, emptyMsg, blocks))
    );
  }

  // ---- turnos list ----
  turnosView() {
    const R = React.createElement;
    const all = this.appts.slice().sort((a, b) => a.day - b.day || this.parseMin(a.start) - this.parseMin(b.start));
    return R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', height: '100%' } },
      this.appbar(),
      R('div', { style: { padding: '2px 18px 12px', flex: '0 0 auto' } },
        R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '26px' } }, 'Turnos'),
        R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', color: '#6F6F73' } }, all.length + ' turnos · junio 2026')),
      R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, overflowY: 'auto', padding: '0 16px 16px', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: '9px' } },
        all.map((a, k) => {
          const s = this.svc(a.service);
          return R('div', { key: k, style: { background: '#1C1C1E', border: '1px solid #2A2A2C', borderRadius: '14px', padding: '13px 14px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '12px' } },
            R('div', { style: { width: '42px', height: '42px', borderRadius: '11px', background: s.bg, border: '1px solid ' + s.bd, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', flex: '0 0 auto' } },
              R('span', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontSize: '13px', fontWeight: 700, color: s.c, lineHeight: 1 } }, a.day),
              R('span', { style: { fontSize: '8px', color: s.c, marginTop: '2px' } }, 'jun')),
            R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minWidth: 0 } },
              R('div', { style: { fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '14px' } }, a.client),
              R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', color: '#ADADB0' } }, a.service)),
            R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '14px', color: '#D9D9DB' } }, a.start));
        }))
    );
  }

  // ---- ganancias stub ----
  gananciasView() {
    const R = React.createElement;
    return R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', height: '100%' } },
      this.appbar(),
      R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', textAlign: 'center', padding: '0 30px', gap: '10px' } },
        R('div', { style: { width: '54px', height: '54px', borderRadius: '15px', background: '#10231B', border: '1px solid #1E4636', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' } }, this.ic('wallet', 26, '#34D399')),
        R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '32px', color: '#34D399' } }, '$52.000'),
        R('div', { style: { fontSize: '13px', color: '#6F6F73', lineHeight: 1.5 } }, 'La pantalla completa de Ganancias\nla diseñamos en su propio paso.'))
    );
  }

  renderScreen() {
    const n = this.state.nav;
    if (n === 'hoy') return this.dayView();
    if (n === 'turnos') return this.turnosView();
    if (n === 'ganancias') return this.gananciasView();
    if (this.state.calView === 'year') return this.yearView();
    if (this.state.calView === 'day') return this.dayView();
    return this.monthView();
  }

  renderVals() {
    const screen = React.createElement('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' } }, this.renderScreen());
    return {
      screen,
      bottomNav: this.buildNav(),
      icArrow: this.ic('arrow', 22, '#2F6BFF'),
      goYear: () => this.setState({ nav: 'agenda', calView: 'year' }),
      goMonth: () => this.setState({ nav: 'agenda', calView: 'month' }),
      goToday: () => this.setState({ nav: 'agenda', calView: 'day', selMonth: 5, selDay: 11 }),
    };
  }
}
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script type="text/x-dc" data-dc-script>
class Component extends DCLogic {
  state = {
    step: 0, services: [], day: 13, time: null, night: false,
    place: null, address: '', name: '', phone: '', email: '', obs: '', code: '',
    product: false, done: false
  };

  // ---- palette ----
  T() {
    return {
      BG: '#0C1322', CARD: '#16213A', SLOT: '#1A2742', BORDER: '#2A3A5E', BSOFT: '#223052',
      TEXT: '#F4F4F2', MUTED: '#9DA9C0', FAINT: '#5F6B85',
      GRAD: 'linear-gradient(135deg,#3B6EF5 0%,#8B5CF6 100%)',
      GLOW: '0 6px 18px -4px rgba(124,92,246,.55)',
      BLUE: '#4D8BFF', GREEN: '#22D366',
      TINT: 'rgba(77,139,255,.10)', TINTBD: '#3D63B0'
    };
  }

  // ---------- icons ----------
  ic(name, size, color) {
    const R = React.createElement;
    const S = (kids) => R('svg', { width: size, height: size, viewBox: '0 0 24 24', fill: 'none', stroke: color, strokeWidth: 2, strokeLinecap: 'round', strokeLinejoin: 'round', style: { display: 'block', flex: '0 0 auto' } }, kids);
    const p = (d, i) => R('path', { key: 'p' + i, d });
    const c = (cx, cy, r, i) => R('circle', { key: 'c' + i, cx, cy, r });
    switch (name) {
      case 'check': return S([p('M20 6 9 17l-5-5', 0)]);
      case 'scissors': return S([c(6, 6, 3, 0), c(6, 18, 3, 1), p('M20 4 8.12 15.88', 2), p('M14.47 14.48 20 20', 3), p('M8.12 8.12 12 12', 4)]);
      case 'pin': return S([p('M20 10c0 6-8 12-8 12s-8-6-8-12a8 8 0 0 1 16 0z', 0), c(12, 10, 3, 1)]);
      case 'user': return S([p('M19 21v-2a4 4 0 0 0-4-4H9a4 4 0 0 0-4 4v2', 0), c(12, 7, 4, 1)]);
      case 'phone': return S([p('M22 16.92v3a2 2 0 0 1-2.18 2 19.8 19.8 0 0 1-8.63-3.07 19.5 19.5 0 0 1-6-6A19.8 19.8 0 0 1 2.1 4.18 2 2 0 0 1 4.1 2h3a2 2 0 0 1 2 1.72c.13.96.36 1.9.7 2.81a2 2 0 0 1-.45 2.11L8.1 9.91a16 16 0 0 0 6 6l1.27-1.27a2 2 0 0 1 2.11-.45c.91.34 1.85.57 2.81.7A2 2 0 0 1 22 16.92z', 0)]);
      case 'mail': return S([p('M4 5h16a1 1 0 0 1 1 1v12a1 1 0 0 1-1 1H4a1 1 0 0 1-1-1V6a1 1 0 0 1 1-1z', 0), p('m3 7 9 6 9-6', 1)]);
      case 'left': return S([p('m15 18-6-6 6-6', 0)]);
      case 'chev-l': return S([p('m15 18-6-6 6-6', 0)]);
      case 'chev-r': return S([p('m9 18 6-6-6-6', 0)]);
      case 'moon': return S([p('M21 12.79A9 9 0 1 1 11.21 3 7 7 0 0 0 21 12.79z', 0)]);
      case 'arrow': return S([c(12, 12, 10, 0), p('M12 8l4 4-4 4', 1), p('M8 12h8', 2)]);
      case 'tag': return S([p('M20.59 13.41 12 22l-8-8V4h10l6.59 6.59a2 2 0 0 1 0 2.82z', 0), c(7.5, 7.5, 1.2, 1)]);
      default: return S([]);
    }
  }

  // ---------- data ----------
  services() {
    return [
      { name: 'Corte de pelo', dur: 40, price: 10000, c: '#34D399' },
      { name: 'Corte + barba', dur: 45, price: 5000, c: '#34D399' },
      { name: 'Coloración', dur: 90, price: 8000, c: '#7FA9FF' },
      { name: 'Claritos', dur: 30, price: 20000, c: '#B79CFF' },
      { name: 'Tratamiento capilar', dur: 60, price: 6000, c: '#E8A33D' },
      { name: 'Peinado', dur: 10, price: 5000, c: '#E8A33D' },
    ];
  }
  daySlots() { return ['09:00', '09:30', '10:00', '10:30', '14:00', '14:30', '15:00', '15:30', '16:00', '16:30', '17:00', '17:30', '18:00', '18:30']; }
  nightSlots() { return ['20:00', '20:30', '21:00', '21:30', '22:00', '22:30']; }
  busy() { return ['10:30', '15:00']; }
  dow(d) { return new Date(2026, 5, d).getDay(); }
  isWeekendNight(d) { return this.dow(d) === 6; }
  wdName(d) { return ['domingo', 'lunes', 'martes', 'miércoles', 'jueves', 'viernes', 'sábado'][this.dow(d)]; }
  money(n) { return '$' + n.toLocaleString('es-AR'); }
  svcList() { return this.services().filter(s => this.state.services.indexOf(s.name) > -1); }
  selDur() { return this.svcList().reduce((a, s) => a + s.dur, 0); }
  selPrice() { return this.svcList().reduce((a, s) => a + s.price, 0); }
  toggleService(name) { const cur = this.state.services.slice(); const i = cur.indexOf(name); if (i > -1) cur.splice(i, 1); else cur.push(name); this.setState({ services: cur }); }

  // ---------- flow ----------
  canNext() {
    const s = this.state;
    if (s.step === 0) return s.services.length > 0;
    if (s.step === 1) return !!s.time;
    if (s.step === 2) return s.place === 'salon' || (s.place === 'home' && s.address.trim() !== '');
    if (s.step === 3) return s.name.trim() !== '' && s.phone.trim() !== '';
    return true;
  }
  next() {
    if (!this.canNext()) return;
    if (this.state.step === 4) this.setState({ done: true });
    else this.setState({ step: this.state.step + 1 });
  }
  goTo(i) { this.setState({ step: i, done: false }); }
  resetState() { return { step: 0, services: [], day: 13, time: null, night: false, place: null, address: '', name: '', phone: '', email: '', obs: '', code: '', product: false, done: false }; }

  // ---------- shared bits ----------
  field(label, icon, node) {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T();
    return R('div', { style: { marginBottom: '13px' } },
      R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', fontWeight: 600, color: t.MUTED, marginBottom: '7px' } }, label),
      R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '10px', background: t.SLOT, border: '1px solid ' + t.BORDER, borderRadius: '12px', padding: '0 13px' } },
        this.ic(icon, 17, t.FAINT), node));
  }
  input(key, ph, type) {
    const t = this.T();
    return React.createElement('input', {
      value: this.state[key], placeholder: ph, type: type || 'text',
      onChange: (e) => this.setState({ [key]: e.target.value }),
      style: { flex: 1, background: 'transparent', border: 0, color: t.TEXT, fontSize: '15px', padding: '13px 0', outline: 'none' }
    });
  }

  doneRow(idx, label, summary) {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T();
    return R('div', {
      key: 'd' + idx,
      style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '11px', padding: '12px 0', borderBottom: '1px solid ' + t.BSOFT }
    },
      R('span', { style: { width: '24px', height: '24px', borderRadius: '50%', background: t.GREEN, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', flex: '0 0 auto' } }, this.ic('check', 14, '#08130D')),
      R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minWidth: 0 } },
        R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', color: t.FAINT, fontWeight: 600 } }, label),
        R('div', { style: { fontSize: '13px', color: '#E4E8F0', fontWeight: 600, whiteSpace: 'nowrap', overflow: 'hidden', textOverflow: 'ellipsis' } }, summary)),
      R('button', { className: 'navbtn', onClick: () => this.goTo(idx), style: { flex: '0 0 auto', background: 'transparent', border: 0, color: t.BLUE, fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '13px', cursor: 'pointer', padding: '4px 8px', borderRadius: '8px' } }, 'Cambiar'));
  }

  activeHead(idx, title, sub) {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T();
    return R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '11px', marginBottom: '16px' } },
      R('span', { style: { width: '27px', height: '27px', borderRadius: '50%', background: t.GRAD, color: '#fff', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontSize: '13px', fontWeight: 700, flex: '0 0 auto', boxShadow: t.GLOW } }, idx + 1),
      R('div', null,
        R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '20px', lineHeight: 1.1 } }, title),
        sub ? R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', color: t.FAINT, marginTop: '2px' } }, sub) : null));
  }

  // ---------- step bodies ----------
  bodyServicio() {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T(), sel = this.state.services;
    const count = sel.length;
    return R('div', null,
      this.services().map((s, i) => {
        const on = sel.indexOf(s.name) > -1;
        return R('button', {
          key: i, className: 'svcitem' + (on ? ' on' : ''), onClick: () => this.toggleService(s.name),
          style: { width: '100%', background: on ? 'rgba(34,211,102,.07)' : t.CARD, border: '2px solid ' + (on ? t.GREEN : t.BSOFT), borderRadius: '14px', padding: '13px 14px', cursor: 'pointer', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '12px', textAlign: 'left', marginBottom: '10px', boxShadow: on ? '0 4px 16px -6px rgba(34,211,102,.4)' : 'none' }
        },
          R('span', { style: { width: '10px', height: '10px', borderRadius: '3px', background: s.c, flex: '0 0 auto' } }),
          R('div', { style: { flex: 1 } },
            R('div', { style: { fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '14.5px', color: '#FFFFFF' } }, s.name),
            R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', color: '#C7D0E0', fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", marginTop: '3px' } }, s.dur + ' min · ' + this.money(s.price))));
      }),
      count > 0 ? R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', marginTop: '4px', padding: '12px 14px', background: t.SLOT, border: '1px solid ' + t.BSOFT, borderRadius: '12px' } },
        R('span', { style: { fontSize: '12px', color: t.MUTED, fontWeight: 600 } }, count + (count === 1 ? ' servicio' : ' servicios') + ' · ' + this.selDur() + ' min'),
        R('span', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '15px', color: t.GREEN } }, this.money(this.selPrice()))) : null);
  }

  bodyFecha() {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T(), s = this.state;
    const wd = ['L', 'M', 'M', 'J', 'V', 'S', 'D'];
    const cells = [];
    for (let d = 1; d <= 30; d++) {
      const past = d < 12, on = s.day === d, today = d === 12;
      cells.push(R('button', {
        key: d, disabled: past, className: 'dcell' + (on ? ' on' : '') + (past ? ' past' : ''),
        onClick: () => this.setState({ day: d, time: null, night: this.isWeekendNight(d) ? s.night : false }),
        style: {
          height: '38px', borderRadius: '10px', cursor: past ? 'default' : 'pointer',
          background: on ? t.GRAD : 'transparent',
          border: today && !on ? '1.5px solid ' + t.BLUE : '1px solid transparent',
          color: past ? '#39455E' : on ? '#fff' : '#E4E8F0',
          fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontSize: '14px', fontWeight: on ? 700 : 500,
          display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
          boxShadow: on ? t.GLOW : 'none'
        }
      }, d));
    }
    const weekendNight = this.isWeekendNight(s.day);
    const slots = (s.night && weekendNight) ? this.nightSlots() : this.daySlots();
    return R('div', null,
      R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: '10px' } },
        R('span', { className: 'navbtn', style: { width: '32px', height: '32px', borderRadius: '9px', background: t.CARD, border: '1px solid ' + t.BSOFT, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', cursor: 'pointer' } }, this.ic('chev-l', 15, t.FAINT)),
        R('span', { style: { fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '15px' } }, 'Junio 2026'),
        R('span', { className: 'navbtn', style: { width: '32px', height: '32px', borderRadius: '9px', background: t.CARD, border: '1px solid ' + t.BSOFT, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', cursor: 'pointer' } }, this.ic('chev-r', 15, t.FAINT))),
      R('div', { style: { display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(7,1fr)', gap: '3px', marginBottom: '4px' } },
        wd.map((w, i) => R('div', { key: i, style: { textAlign: 'center', fontSize: '11px', fontWeight: 700, color: t.FAINT, padding: '4px 0' } }, w))),
      R('div', { style: { display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(7,1fr)', gap: '3px', marginBottom: '14px' } }, cells),
      // nocturno — solo Vie/Sáb
      weekendNight ? R('button', {
        onClick: () => this.setState({ night: !s.night, time: null }),
        style: { width: '100%', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '11px', background: s.night ? 'rgba(124,92,246,.14)' : t.CARD, border: '1px solid ' + (s.night ? '#6D4FCF' : t.BSOFT), borderRadius: '13px', padding: '12px 14px', cursor: 'pointer', textAlign: 'left', marginBottom: '16px' }
      },
        R('span', { style: { width: '34px', height: '34px', borderRadius: '9px', background: s.night ? 'rgba(124,92,246,.22)' : t.SLOT, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', flex: '0 0 auto' } }, this.ic('moon', 17, s.night ? '#B79CFF' : t.MUTED)),
        R('div', { style: { flex: 1 } },
          R('div', { style: { fontSize: '13px', fontWeight: 700, color: s.night ? '#C4B0FF' : t.TEXT } }, 'Horario nocturno especial'),
          R('div', { style: { fontSize: '11px', color: s.night ? '#9B85D6' : t.FAINT } }, '20:00 – 23:00 · salís directo a bailar')),
        R('span', { style: { width: '42px', height: '24px', borderRadius: '999px', background: s.night ? t.GRAD : '#33405E', position: 'relative', flex: '0 0 auto', transition: 'background .15s', boxShadow: s.night ? t.GLOW : 'none' } },
          R('span', { style: { position: 'absolute', top: '2px', left: s.night ? '20px' : '2px', width: '20px', height: '20px', borderRadius: '50%', background: '#fff', transition: 'left .15s' } }))) : null,
      R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', fontWeight: 600, color: t.MUTED, marginBottom: '10px' } }, 'Horarios disponibles — ' + this.wdName(s.day) + ' ' + s.day + ' de junio'),
      R('div', { style: { display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(4,1fr)', gap: '8px' } },
        slots.map((tm, i) => {
          const isBusy = this.busy().indexOf(tm) > -1, on = s.time === tm;
          if (isBusy) return R('div', { key: i, className: 'tslot busy', style: { textAlign: 'center', padding: '13px 0', borderRadius: '11px', background: '#121B2E', border: '1px solid ' + t.BSOFT, color: '#3B4763', fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontSize: '13px', textDecoration: 'line-through' } }, tm);
          return R('button', { key: i, className: 'tslot' + (on ? ' on' : ''), onClick: () => this.setState({ time: tm }), style: { textAlign: 'center', padding: '13px 0', borderRadius: '11px', background: on ? t.GRAD : t.SLOT, border: '1px solid ' + (on ? 'transparent' : t.BORDER), color: on ? '#fff' : '#E4E8F0', fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontSize: '13px', fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer', boxShadow: on ? t.GLOW : 'none' } }, tm);
        })));
  }

  bodyLugar() {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T(), s = this.state;
    const opt = (key, emoji, title, sub) => {
      const on = s.place === key;
      return R('button', {
        key: key, className: 'optcard' + (on ? ' on' : ''), onClick: () => this.setState({ place: key }),
        style: { flex: 1, background: on ? t.TINT : t.CARD, border: '1px solid ' + (on ? t.BLUE : t.BSOFT), borderRadius: '15px', padding: '16px 13px', cursor: 'pointer', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: '9px', textAlign: 'left' }
      },
        R('span', { style: { width: '42px', height: '42px', borderRadius: '11px', background: on ? 'rgba(77,139,255,.16)' : t.SLOT, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', fontSize: '23px', lineHeight: 1 } }, emoji),
        R('span', { style: { fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '14px', color: t.TEXT } }, title),
        R('span', { style: { fontSize: '11px', color: t.MUTED, lineHeight: 1.4 } }, sub));
    };
    return R('div', null,
      R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', gap: '11px', marginBottom: '14px' } },
        opt('salon', '🏪', 'En el local', 'Venís a la peluquería.'),
        opt('home', '🏠', 'A domicilio', 'Vamos a tu dirección.')),
      s.place === 'home'
        ? R('div', null,
          R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', gap: '9px', alignItems: 'flex-start', background: 'rgba(232,163,61,.10)', border: '1px solid #6E5224', borderRadius: '12px', padding: '11px 13px', marginBottom: '13px' } },
            R('span', { style: { color: '#E8A33D', fontSize: '14px', flex: '0 0 auto', lineHeight: 1.3 } }, '⚠'),
            R('span', { style: { fontSize: '12px', color: '#E8A33D', lineHeight: 1.5 } }, 'Tené en cuenta que puede haber un adicional según la distancia.')),
          this.field('Dirección completa', 'pin', this.input('address', 'Calle, número, piso…')))
        : s.place === 'salon'
          ? R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', color: t.FAINT, textAlign: 'center', padding: '6px' } }, 'Te esperamos en BarberFras 💈')
          : R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', color: t.FAINT, textAlign: 'center', padding: '6px' } }, 'Elegí una opción para continuar.'));
  }

  bodyDatos() {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T(), s = this.state;
    return R('div', null,
      this.field('Nombre completo *', 'user', this.input('name', 'Ej: Juan Pérez')),
      this.field('Teléfono / WhatsApp *', 'phone', this.input('phone', 'Ej: 11 2345 6789', 'tel')),
      this.field('Email (opcional)', 'mail', this.input('email', 'tucorreo@mail.com', 'email')),
      R('div', { style: { marginBottom: '13px' } },
        R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', fontWeight: 600, color: t.MUTED, marginBottom: '7px' } }, 'Observaciones (opcional)'),
        R('textarea', { value: s.obs, onChange: (e) => this.setState({ obs: e.target.value }), placeholder: 'Algo que quieras aclarar…', rows: 3, style: { width: '100%', background: t.SLOT, border: '1px solid ' + t.BORDER, borderRadius: '12px', color: t.TEXT, fontSize: '15px', padding: '12px 13px', outline: 'none', resize: 'none' } })),
      R('div', null,
        R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', fontWeight: 600, color: t.MUTED, marginBottom: '7px' } }, 'Código de descuento (opcional)'),
        R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', gap: '8px' } },
          R('div', { style: { flex: 1, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '10px', background: t.SLOT, border: '1px solid ' + t.BORDER, borderRadius: '12px', padding: '0 13px' } },
            this.ic('tag', 16, t.FAINT),
            R('input', { value: s.code, onChange: (e) => this.setState({ code: e.target.value }), placeholder: 'XXXXX', style: { flex: 1, background: 'transparent', border: 0, color: t.TEXT, fontSize: '15px', padding: '13px 0', outline: 'none', letterSpacing: '.08em' } })),
          R('button', { className: 'navbtn', style: { flex: '0 0 auto', borderRadius: '12px', background: t.CARD, color: t.TEXT, border: '1px solid ' + t.BORDER, fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '14px', padding: '0 18px', cursor: 'pointer' } }, 'Aplicar'))));
  }

  bodyResumen() {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T(), s = this.state;
    const total = this.selPrice() + (s.product ? 10000 : 0);
    return R('div', null,
      R('div', { style: { textAlign: 'center', marginBottom: '14px' } },
        R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '19px', lineHeight: 1.2 } }, '¿Querés agregar productos?'),
        R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', color: t.FAINT, marginTop: '3px' } }, 'Llevate algo para mantener tu estilo en casa.')),
      R('button', {
        className: 'optcard' + (s.product ? ' on' : ''), onClick: () => this.setState({ product: !s.product }),
        style: { width: '100%', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '12px', background: s.product ? t.TINT : t.CARD, border: '1px solid ' + (s.product ? t.BLUE : t.BSOFT), borderRadius: '14px', padding: '13px', cursor: 'pointer', textAlign: 'left', marginBottom: '16px' }
      },
        R('span', { style: { width: '46px', height: '46px', borderRadius: '10px', background: t.SLOT, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', fontSize: '22px', flex: '0 0 auto' } }, '🫙'),
        R('div', { style: { flex: 1 } },
          R('div', { style: { fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '14px' } }, 'Pomada'),
          R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', color: t.FAINT } }, 'Peinate para adentro'),
          R('div', { style: { fontSize: '13px', fontWeight: 700, color: t.GREEN, fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", marginTop: '2px' } }, this.money(10000))),
        R('span', { style: { width: '22px', height: '22px', borderRadius: '7px', background: s.product ? t.GREEN : 'transparent', border: s.product ? '0' : '1.5px solid ' + t.BORDER, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', flex: '0 0 auto', boxShadow: s.product ? '0 4px 12px -3px rgba(34,211,102,.5)' : 'none' } }, s.product ? this.ic('check', 13, '#08130D') : null)),
      R('div', { style: { borderTop: '1px solid ' + t.BSOFT, paddingTop: '12px' } },
        this.svcList().map((sv, i) => R('div', { key: i, style: { display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', fontSize: '13px', color: t.MUTED, marginBottom: '6px' } },
          R('span', null, sv.name), R('span', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace" } }, this.money(sv.price)))),
        s.product ? R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', fontSize: '13px', color: t.MUTED, marginBottom: '6px' } },
          R('span', null, 'Pomada'), R('span', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace" } }, this.money(10000))) : null,
        R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', marginTop: '8px' } },
          R('span', { style: { fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '14px' } }, 'Total estimado'),
          R('span', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '21px', color: t.GREEN } }, this.money(total)))));
  }

  // ---------- assembly ----------
  summaryFor(idx) {
    const s = this.state;
    if (idx === 0) { const l = this.svcList(); return l.length ? l.map(x => x.name).join(' + ') + ' · ' + this.selDur() + ' min · ' + this.money(this.selPrice()) : ''; }
    if (idx === 1) return this.wdName(s.day) + ' ' + s.day + ' de junio a las ' + (s.time || '');
    if (idx === 2) return s.place === 'home' ? 'A domicilio · ' + (s.address || 'sin dirección') : 'Presencial en el local';
    if (idx === 3) return s.name + (s.phone ? ' · ' + s.phone : '');
    return '';
  }

  // confirmation rows (emoji con color + ícono propio en ubicación)
  infoRow(visual, label, value, sub) {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T();
    const inner = typeof visual === 'string' ? R('span', { style: { fontSize: '21px', lineHeight: 1 } }, visual) : visual;
    return R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', gap: '13px', alignItems: 'flex-start', padding: '14px 0', borderBottom: '1px solid ' + t.BSOFT } },
      R('span', { style: { width: '40px', height: '40px', borderRadius: '11px', background: t.SLOT, border: '1px solid ' + t.BSOFT, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', flex: '0 0 auto' } }, inner),
      R('div', null,
        R('div', { style: { fontSize: '11px', fontWeight: 700, letterSpacing: '.1em', color: t.FAINT } }, label),
        R('div', { style: { fontSize: '15px', fontWeight: 700, marginTop: '2px' } }, value),
        sub ? R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', color: t.MUTED, marginTop: '1px' } }, sub) : null));
  }

  doneScreen() {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T(), s = this.state, l = this.svcList();
    const total = this.selPrice() + (s.product ? 10000 : 0);
    return R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, overflowY: 'auto', background: t.BG, padding: '18px' } },
      // tarjeta inset con marco redondito
      R('div', { style: { borderRadius: '24px', overflow: 'hidden', border: '1px solid ' + t.BORDER, background: t.CARD, boxShadow: '0 24px 60px -28px rgba(0,0,0,.8)' } },
        R('div', { style: { background: 'linear-gradient(160deg,#1B7A53,#0E6B47)', padding: '30px 24px 26px', textAlign: 'center' } },
          R('div', { style: { width: '58px', height: '58px', borderRadius: '50%', background: 'rgba(255,255,255,.18)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', margin: '0 auto 13px' } }, this.ic('check', 28, '#fff')),
          R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '25px', color: '#fff' } }, 'BarberFras'),
          R('div', { style: { fontSize: '14px', color: 'rgba(255,255,255,.85)', marginTop: '4px' } }, 'Tu turno está confirmado')),
        R('div', { style: { padding: '6px 20px 20px' } },
          this.infoRow('✂️', 'SERVICIO', l.length ? l.map(x => x.name).join(' + ') : '—', l.length ? (l.length === 1 ? '1 servicio' : l.length + ' servicios') + ' · ' + this.selDur() + ' min' : ''),
          this.infoRow('📅', 'FECHA Y HORA', this.wdName(s.day) + ' ' + s.day + ' de junio', s.time || ''),
          this.infoRow(this.ic('pin', 21, t.BLUE), 'UBICACIÓN', s.place === 'home' ? 'A domicilio' : 'En el local', s.place === 'home' ? (s.address || 'Dirección cargada') : 'BarberFras'),
          this.infoRow('💈', 'PRODUCTOS', s.product ? '1 producto seleccionado' : 'Sin productos', s.product ? 'Pomada · ' + this.money(10000) : null),
          R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', padding: '16px 2px 16px' } },
            R('span', { style: { fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '14px' } }, 'Total estimado'),
            R('span', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '20px', color: t.GREEN } }, this.money(total))),
          R('button', { className: 'ctabtn', onClick: () => this.setState(this.resetState()), style: { width: '100%', borderRadius: '13px', background: t.SLOT, border: '1px solid ' + t.BORDER, color: t.TEXT, fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '14px', padding: '14px', cursor: 'pointer' } }, 'Reservar otro turno'))));
  }

  renderForm() {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T(), s = this.state;
    if (s.done) return this.doneScreen();

    const meta = [
      { label: 'Servicio', title: 'Elegí el servicio', sub: 'Podés elegir más de uno.' },
      { label: 'Fecha y horario', title: 'Elegí fecha y horario', sub: 'Solo mostramos horarios libres.' },
      { label: 'Modalidad', title: '¿Cómo querés el turno?', sub: 'En el local o a domicilio.' },
      { label: 'Tus datos', title: 'Tus datos', sub: 'Para confirmar y avisarte.' },
      { label: 'Confirmar', title: 'Revisá y confirmá', sub: 'Último paso.' },
    ];
    const bodies = [this.bodyServicio(), this.bodyFecha(), this.bodyLugar(), this.bodyDatos(), this.bodyResumen()];
    const can = this.canNext();

    const header = R('div', { style: { flex: '0 0 auto', background: t.BG, borderBottom: '1px solid #16203A', padding: '10px 18px 12px' } },
      R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '10px', marginBottom: '11px' } },
        R('span', { style: { width: '34px', height: '34px', borderRadius: '9px', background: t.CARD, border: '1px solid ' + t.BORDER, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', flex: '0 0 auto' } }, this.ic('scissors', 17, '#7C9CFF')),
        R('div', { style: { flex: 1 } },
          R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '16px', lineHeight: 1 } }, 'BarberFras'),
          R('div', { style: { fontSize: '11px', color: t.FAINT, marginTop: '2px' } }, 'Reservar turno')),
        R('span', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontSize: '12px', color: t.FAINT } }, (s.step + 1) + '/5')),
      R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', gap: '5px' } },
        [0, 1, 2, 3, 4].map(i => R('span', { key: i, style: { flex: 1, height: '4px', borderRadius: '2px', background: i <= s.step ? t.GRAD : '#23304E', transition: 'background .2s' } }))));

    const stack = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < s.step; i++) stack.push(this.doneRow(i, meta[i].label, this.summaryFor(i)));
    stack.push(R('div', { key: 'active', style: { paddingTop: s.step > 0 ? '14px' : '2px' } },
      this.activeHead(s.step, meta[s.step].title, meta[s.step].sub),
      bodies[s.step]));

    const scroll = R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, overflowY: 'auto', background: t.BG } },
      R('div', { style: { maxWidth: '460px', margin: '0 auto', width: '100%', padding: '14px 18px 18px' } }, stack));

    const footer = R('div', { style: { flex: '0 0 auto', padding: '12px 18px 20px', borderTop: '1px solid #16203A', background: t.BG } },
      R('div', { style: { maxWidth: '460px', margin: '0 auto', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: '8px' } },
        R('button', { className: 'ctabtn', onClick: () => this.next(), disabled: !can, style: { width: '100%', border: 0, borderRadius: '14px', background: can ? t.GRAD : '#1A2742', color: can ? '#fff' : '#46557A', fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '15px', padding: '15px', cursor: can ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed', boxShadow: can ? t.GLOW : 'none' } }, s.step === 4 ? 'Confirmar reserva' : 'Continuar'),
        s.step === 4 ? R('button', { onClick: () => this.setState({ product: false, done: true }), style: { width: '100%', border: 0, background: 'transparent', color: t.FAINT, fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '13px', padding: '4px', cursor: 'pointer' } }, 'Omitir y confirmar sin productos') : null));

    return R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', background: t.BG } }, header, scroll, footer);
  }

  renderVals() {
    return {
      screen: this.renderForm(),
      icArrow: this.ic('arrow', 22, '#7C9CFF'),
      reset: () => this.setState(this.resetState()),
    };
  }
}
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script type="text/x-dc" data-dc-script>
class Component extends DCLogic {
  state = { periodA: 'year', periodB: 'year' };

  T() {
    return {
      BG: '#131313', CARD: '#1C1C1E', BD: '#2A2A2C', BD2: '#38383B',
      TEXT: '#F4F4F2', MUTED: '#ADADB0', FAINT: '#6F6F73',
      BLUE: '#2F6BFF', GREEN: '#22D366', YELLOW: '#E8A33D', RED: '#F26157', PURPLE: '#B79CFF',
    };
  }

  money(n) { return '$' + n.toLocaleString('es-AR'); }
  moneyK(n) { return n >= 1000 ? '$' + (n / 1000).toFixed(0) + 'K' : '$' + n; }

  ic(name, size, color) {
    const R = React.createElement;
    const S = (kids) => R('svg', { width: size, height: size, viewBox: '0 0 24 24', fill: 'none', stroke: color, strokeWidth: 2, strokeLinecap: 'round', strokeLinejoin: 'round', style: { display: 'block', flex: '0 0 auto' } }, kids);
    const p = (d, i) => R('path', { key: 'p' + i, d });
    const c = (cx, cy, r, i) => R('circle', { key: 'c' + i, cx, cy, r });
    switch (name) {
      case 'home': return S([p('M3 9l9-7 9 7v11a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V9z', 0), p('M9 22V12h6v10', 1)]);
      case 'cal': return S([R('rect', { key: 'r', x: 3, y: 4, width: 18, height: 18, rx: 2 }), p('M16 2v4', 1), p('M8 2v4', 2), p('M3 10h18', 3)]);
      case 'wallet': return S([p('M21 12V7a2 2 0 0 0-2-2H5a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v10a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h14a2 2 0 0 0 2-2v-5z', 0), p('M16 12a1 1 0 1 0 0 2 1 1 0 0 0 0-2z', 1)]);
      case 'trending': return S([p('M23 6l-9.5 9.5-5-5L1 18', 0), p('M17 6h6v6', 1)]);
      case 'arrow': return S([c(12, 12, 10, 0), p('M12 8l4 4-4 4', 1), p('M8 12h8', 2)]);
      default: return S([]);
    }
  }

  monthlyData() {
    return [
      { m: 'E', total: 45000, cortes: 12 }, { m: 'F', total: 52000, cortes: 14 },
      { m: 'M', total: 38000, cortes: 10 }, { m: 'A', total: 61000, cortes: 16 },
      { m: 'M', total: 55000, cortes: 15 }, { m: 'J', total: 68000, cortes: 18 },
      { m: 'J', total: 0, cortes: 0 }, { m: 'A', total: 0, cortes: 0 },
      { m: 'S', total: 0, cortes: 0 }, { m: 'O', total: 0, cortes: 0 },
      { m: 'N', total: 0, cortes: 0 }, { m: 'D', total: 0, cortes: 0 },
    ];
  }

  serviceData() {
    return [
      { name: 'Corte', total: 120000, count: 32, color: '#22D366' },
      { name: 'C+Barba', total: 85000, count: 18, color: '#2F6BFF' },
      { name: 'Color', total: 72000, count: 9, color: '#B79CFF' },
      { name: 'Claritos', total: 60000, count: 3, color: '#E8A33D' },
      { name: 'Tratam.', total: 42000, count: 7, color: '#F26157' },
      { name: 'Peinado', total: 25000, count: 5, color: '#6F6F73' },
    ];
  }

  // ---- period-aware data ----
  periodBarData(period) {
    if (period === 'week') return [
      { m: 'Lun', total: 15000, cortes: 4, isCurrent: false },
      { m: 'Mar', total: 8000, cortes: 2, isCurrent: false },
      { m: 'Mié', total: 22000, cortes: 6, isCurrent: false },
      { m: 'Jue', total: 20000, cortes: 5, isCurrent: false },
      { m: 'Vie', total: 31000, cortes: 8, isCurrent: false },
      { m: 'Sáb', total: 28000, cortes: 7, isCurrent: false },
      { m: 'Hoy', total: 10000, cortes: 2, isCurrent: true },
    ];
    if (period === 'month') return [
      { m: 'S1', total: 68000, cortes: 18, isCurrent: false },
      { m: 'S2', total: 75000, cortes: 20, isCurrent: false },
      { m: 'S3', total: 82000, cortes: 22, isCurrent: false },
      { m: 'S4', total: 43000, cortes: 12, isCurrent: true },
    ];
    return this.monthlyData().map((d, i) => ({ ...d, isCurrent: i === 5 }));
  }

  periodStats(period) {
    const data = this.periodBarData(period);
    const total = data.reduce((a, d) => a + d.total, 0);
    const cortes = data.reduce((a, d) => a + d.cortes, 0);
    const ticket = cortes ? Math.round(total / cortes) : 0;
    const trends = { week: '+18% vs sem. ant.', month: '+8% vs mayo', year: '+12% vs 2025' };
    const chartLabels = { week: 'ESTA SEMANA', month: 'JUNIO · POR SEMANA', year: 'EVOLUCIÓN MENSUAL · 2026' };
    const heroLabels = { week: 'TOTAL · ESTA SEMANA', month: 'TOTAL · JUNIO 2026', year: 'TOTAL COBRADO · 2026' };
    return { total, cortes, ticket, trend: trends[period], chartLabel: chartLabels[period], heroLabel: heroLabels[period] };
  }

  periodServiceData(period) {
    const scale = period === 'week' ? 0.035 : period === 'month' ? 0.42 : 1;
    return this.serviceData().map(s => ({ ...s, total: Math.round(s.total * scale), count: Math.max(0, Math.round(s.count * scale)) }));
  }

  // ---- SVG: barras verticales (period-aware) ----
  periodBarChart(data, width, height) {
    const R = React.createElement;
    const max = Math.max(...data.map(d => d.total)) || 1;
    const chartH = height - 14;
    const slot = Math.floor(width / data.length);
    const barW = Math.max(6, slot - 4);

    return R('svg', { width, height, viewBox: '0 0 ' + width + ' ' + height, style: { display: 'block', overflow: 'visible' } },
      R('defs', null,
        R('linearGradient', { id: 'mBarGrad', x1: '0%', y1: '0%', x2: '0%', y2: '100%' },
          R('stop', { offset: '0%', stopColor: '#22D366' }),
          R('stop', { offset: '100%', stopColor: '#2F6BFF', stopOpacity: 0.6 }))),
      data.map((d, i) => {
        const isFuture = d.total === 0;
        const isCurrent = d.isCurrent;
        const barH = isFuture ? 2 : Math.max(3, Math.round((d.total / max) * chartH));
        const x = i * slot + 2;
        const y = chartH - barH;
        return R('g', { key: i },
          R('rect', { x, y: isFuture ? chartH - 2 : y, width: barW, height: isFuture ? 2 : barH, rx: 3, fill: isFuture ? '#222' : isCurrent ? 'url(#mBarGrad)' : '#243652' }),
          R('text', { x: x + barW / 2, y: height - 1, textAnchor: 'middle', fill: isCurrent ? '#7CB9FF' : '#404048', fontSize: '7', fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono, monospace' }, d.m));
      }));
  }

  // ---- SVG: barras verticales por servicio ----
  serviceBarChartV(data, width, height) {
    const R = React.createElement;
    const max = Math.max(...data.map(d => d.total));
    const chartH = height - 22;
    const slot = Math.floor(width / data.length);
    const barW = slot - 6;

    return R('svg', { width, height, viewBox: '0 0 ' + width + ' ' + height, style: { display: 'block', overflow: 'visible' } },
      data.map((d, i) => {
        const barH = Math.max(3, Math.round((d.total / max) * chartH));
        const x = i * slot + 3;
        const y = chartH - barH;
        return R('g', { key: i },
          R('rect', { x, y, width: barW, height: barH, rx: 3, fill: d.color, opacity: 0.88 }),
          R('text', { x: x + barW / 2, y: chartH + 11, textAnchor: 'middle', fill: d.color, opacity: 0.8, fontSize: '7.5', fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono, monospace' }, d.name),
          R('text', { x: x + barW / 2, y: chartH + 21, textAnchor: 'middle', fill: '#4A4A50', fontSize: '7', fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono, monospace' }, this.moneyK(d.total)));
      }));
  }

  // ---- SVG: barras horizontales por servicio (Variation B) ----
  serviceBarChartH(width, height) {
    const R = React.createElement;
    const data = this.serviceData();
    const max = Math.max(...data.map(d => d.total));
    const rowH = Math.floor(height / data.length);
    const labelW = 46;
    const valW = 30;
    const barAreaW = width - labelW - valW - 6;

    return R('svg', { width, height, viewBox: '0 0 ' + width + ' ' + height, style: { display: 'block' } },
      data.map((d, i) => {
        const barW = Math.max(4, Math.round((d.total / max) * barAreaW));
        const y = i * rowH + 2;
        const bH = Math.max(8, rowH - 5);
        return R('g', { key: i },
          R('text', { x: 0, y: y + bH * 0.72, fill: '#9C9CA0', fontSize: '8', fontFamily: 'Manrope, sans-serif', fontWeight: 600 }, d.name),
          R('rect', { x: labelW, y: y + 1, width: barAreaW, height: bH - 2, rx: 3, fill: '#1A1A1C' }),
          R('rect', { x: labelW, y: y + 1, width: barW, height: bH - 2, rx: 3, fill: d.color, opacity: 0.85 }),
          R('text', { x: labelW + barAreaW + 4, y: y + bH * 0.72, fill: d.color, fontSize: '7.5', fontFamily: 'JetBrains Mono, monospace', fontWeight: 700 }, this.moneyK(d.total)));
      }));
  }

  // ---- SVG: sparkline (period-aware) ----
  sparkline(rawData, width, height) {
    const R = React.createElement;
    const data = rawData.filter(d => d.total > 0);
    if (data.length < 2) return R('div', null);
    const max = Math.max(...data.map(d => d.total));
    const chartH = height - 4;
    const stepX = (width - 10) / (data.length - 1);
    const pts = data.map((d, i) => ({ x: 5 + i * stepX, y: chartH - Math.round((d.total / max) * (chartH - 4)) }));
    const poly = pts.map(p => p.x + ',' + p.y).join(' ');
    const area = 'M ' + pts[0].x + ' ' + (chartH + 2) + ' L ' + pts.map(p => p.x + ' ' + p.y).join(' L ') + ' L ' + pts[pts.length - 1].x + ' ' + (chartH + 2) + ' Z';
    return R('svg', { width, height, viewBox: '0 0 ' + width + ' ' + height, style: { display: 'block' } },
      R('defs', null,
        R('linearGradient', { id: 'spArea', x1: '0%', y1: '0%', x2: '0%', y2: '100%' },
          R('stop', { offset: '0%', stopColor: '#22D366', stopOpacity: 0.28 }),
          R('stop', { offset: '100%', stopColor: '#22D366', stopOpacity: 0 }))),
      R('path', { d: area, fill: 'url(#spArea)' }),
      R('polyline', { points: poly, fill: 'none', stroke: '#22D366', strokeWidth: 1.8, strokeLinejoin: 'round', strokeLinecap: 'round' }),
      pts.map((p, i) => R('circle', { key: i, cx: p.x, cy: p.y, r: i === pts.length - 1 ? 3.5 : 2, fill: '#131313', stroke: '#22D366', strokeWidth: 2 })));
  }

  buildNav() {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T();
    const items = [
      { key: 'home', label: 'Inicio', icon: 'home' },
      { key: 'turnos', label: 'Turnos', icon: 'cal', dot: true },
      { key: 'ganancias', label: 'Ganancias', icon: 'wallet', active: true },
    ];
    return R('div', { style: { flex: '0 0 auto', display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-around', padding: '8px 0 18px', borderTop: '1px solid #1E1E20', background: t.BG } },
      items.map(it =>
        R('div', { key: it.key, className: 'navitem', style: { display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', gap: '3px', position: 'relative', padding: '2px 12px 0' } },
          R('div', { style: { position: 'relative', display: 'flex' } },
            this.ic(it.icon, 22, it.active ? t.BLUE : t.FAINT),
            it.dot ? R('span', { style: { position: 'absolute', top: '-2px', right: '-5px', width: '9px', height: '9px', borderRadius: '50%', background: t.GREEN, border: '2px solid ' + t.BG } }) : null),
          R('span', { style: { fontSize: '10px', fontWeight: it.active ? 700 : 500, color: it.active ? t.BLUE : t.FAINT } }, it.label))));
  }

  periodChips(currentPeriod, stateKey, accentColor) {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T();
    return R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', gap: '6px', marginBottom: '12px' } },
      ['week', 'month', 'year'].map(p => {
        const on = currentPeriod === p;
        return R('button', {
          key: p, className: 'pchip',
          onClick: () => this.setState({ [stateKey]: p }),
          style: { border: on ? '1px solid ' + accentColor + '55' : '1px solid transparent', borderRadius: '20px', padding: '5px 12px', fontSize: '11px', fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer', background: on ? accentColor + '18' : t.CARD, color: on ? accentColor : t.FAINT }
        }, p === 'week' ? 'Semana' : p === 'month' ? 'Mes' : 'Año');
      }));
  }

  recentList(t) {
    const R = React.createElement;
    return R('div', null,
      R('div', { style: { fontSize: '10px', fontWeight: 700, color: t.FAINT, letterSpacing: '.09em', marginBottom: '8px' } }, 'ÚLTIMOS COBRADOS'),
      this.recentCobros().map(c =>
        R('div', { key: c.id, style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '10px', padding: '9px 0', borderBottom: '1px solid #1A1A1C' } },
          R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minWidth: 0 } },
            R('div', { style: { fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '13px', color: t.TEXT, whiteSpace: 'nowrap', overflow: 'hidden', textOverflow: 'ellipsis' } }, c.name),
            R('div', { style: { fontSize: '11px', color: t.MUTED, marginTop: '1px' } }, c.service + ' · ' + c.day)),
          R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '13px', color: t.GREEN, flex: '0 0 auto' } }, this.money(c.price)))));
  }

  // =================== SCREEN A (period-aware) ===================
  screenA() {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T();
    const period = this.state.periodA;
    const stats = this.periodStats(period);
    const barData = this.periodBarData(period);
    const svcData = this.periodServiceData(period);

    return R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' } },
      R('div', { style: { padding: '8px 18px 0', flex: '0 0 auto' } },
        R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: '10px' } },
          R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '24px' } }, 'Ganancias'),
          R('span', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontSize: '12px', color: t.FAINT } }, '2026')),
        this.periodChips(period, 'periodA', t.GREEN),
        // blue hero card (sparkline)
        R('div', { style: { background: 'linear-gradient(145deg,#182238,#0F1827)', border: '1px solid #253450', borderRadius: '18px', padding: '13px 15px 11px', marginBottom: '12px' } },
          R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: '3px' } },
            R('div', { style: { fontSize: '10px', fontWeight: 700, color: '#5F7BAD', letterSpacing: '.1em' } }, stats.heroLabel),
            R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '4px' } },
              this.ic('trending', 12, t.GREEN),
              R('span', { style: { fontSize: '11px', fontWeight: 700, color: t.GREEN, fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace" } }, stats.trend))),
          R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontWeight: 800, fontSize: '26px', color: '#fff', lineHeight: 1, marginBottom: '10px' } }, this.money(stats.total)),
          this.sparkline(barData, 266, 48)),
        // stat chips
        R('div', { style: { display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: '1fr 1fr', gap: '7px', marginBottom: '12px' } },
          [
            { label: 'CORTES', value: stats.cortes + ' cortes', color: t.TEXT },
            { label: 'TICKET PROM.', value: this.money(stats.ticket), color: t.BLUE },
          ].map((s, i) =>
            R('div', { key: i, style: { background: t.CARD, border: '1px solid ' + t.BD, borderRadius: '11px', padding: '9px 11px' } },
              R('div', { style: { fontSize: '9px', fontWeight: 700, color: t.FAINT, letterSpacing: '.08em', marginBottom: '3px' } }, s.label),
              R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '13px', color: s.color } }, s.value)))),
        // period bar chart
        R('div', { style: { background: t.CARD, border: '1px solid ' + t.BD, borderRadius: '13px', padding: '10px 12px 8px' } },
          R('div', { style: { fontSize: '10px', fontWeight: 700, color: t.FAINT, letterSpacing: '.08em', marginBottom: '8px' } }, stats.chartLabel),
          this.periodBarChart(barData, 266, 68))),
      // scrollable: service chart
      R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, overflowY: 'auto', padding: '12px 18px 18px' } },
        R('div', { style: { background: t.CARD, border: '1px solid ' + t.BD, borderRadius: '13px', padding: '10px 12px 6px' } },
          R('div', { style: { fontSize: '10px', fontWeight: 700, color: t.FAINT, letterSpacing: '.08em', marginBottom: '8px' } }, 'GANANCIA POR SERVICIO'),
          this.serviceBarChartV(svcData, 266, 96))));
  }

  // =================== SCREEN B ===================
  screenB() {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T();
    return R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' } },
      R('div', { style: { padding: '8px 18px 0', flex: '0 0 auto' } },
        R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: '10px' } },
          R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '24px' } }, 'Ganancias'),
          R('span', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontSize: '12px', color: t.FAINT } }, '2026')),
        this.periodChips(this.state.periodB, 'periodB', t.BLUE),
        // hero card
        R('div', { style: { background: 'linear-gradient(145deg,#182238,#0F1827)', border: '1px solid #253450', borderRadius: '18px', padding: '14px 16px 10px', marginBottom: '12px' } },
          R('div', { style: { fontSize: '10px', fontWeight: 700, color: '#5F7BAD', letterSpacing: '.1em', marginBottom: '3px' } }, 'TOTAL · ESTE AÑO'),
          R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontWeight: 800, fontSize: '26px', color: '#fff', lineHeight: 1, marginBottom: '8px' } }, this.money(this.totalYear())),
          R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', gap: '18px', marginBottom: '10px' } },
            [
              { label: 'CORTES', value: this.totalCortes() },
              { label: 'TICKET', value: this.money(this.ticketProm()) },
              { label: 'TREND', value: '+12%' },
            ].map((s, i) =>
              R('div', { key: i },
                R('div', { style: { fontSize: '9px', color: '#4A6490', fontWeight: 700, letterSpacing: '.06em' } }, s.label),
                R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '13px', color: i === 2 ? t.GREEN : '#9DB4FF', marginTop: '2px' } }, s.value)))),
          this.monthlySparkline(266, 42))),
      // scrollable
      R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, overflowY: 'auto', padding: '0 18px 18px' } },
        // top service badge
        R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '10px', background: t.CARD, border: '1px solid ' + t.BD, borderRadius: '13px', padding: '11px 13px', marginBottom: '12px' } },
          R('span', { style: { fontSize: '20px', flex: '0 0 auto' } }, '🏆'),
          R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minWidth: 0 } },
            R('div', { style: { fontSize: '10px', fontWeight: 700, color: t.FAINT, letterSpacing: '.08em' } }, 'SERVICIO MÁS VENDIDO'),
            R('div', { style: { fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '14px', color: t.TEXT, marginTop: '2px' } }, 'Corte de pelo'),
            R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace", fontSize: '12px', color: t.GREEN } }, this.money(this.topService().total))),
          R('div', { style: { textAlign: 'right', flex: '0 0 auto' } },
            R('div', { style: { fontSize: '10px', color: t.FAINT, fontFamily: "'JetBrains Mono',monospace" } }, this.topService().count + ' cortes'))),
        // horizontal bars
        R('div', { style: { background: t.CARD, border: '1px solid ' + t.BD, borderRadius: '13px', padding: '11px 13px 10px', marginBottom: '14px' } },
          R('div', { style: { fontSize: '10px', fontWeight: 700, color: t.FAINT, letterSpacing: '.08em', marginBottom: '10px' } }, 'GANANCIA POR SERVICIO'),
          this.serviceBarChartH(266, 108)),
        this.recentList(t)));
  }

  renderVals() {
    const screenA = React.createElement('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' } }, this.screenA());
    return {
      screenA,
      navA: this.buildNav(),
      icArrow: this.ic('arrow', 22, '#2F6BFF'),
    };
  }
}
</script>
</body>
</html>

    const p = (d, i) => R('path', { key: 'p' + i, d });
    const c = (cx, cy, r, i) => R('circle', { key: 'c' + i, cx, cy, r });
    switch (name) {
      case 'menu': return S([p('M3 12h18', 0), p('M3 6h18', 1), p('M3 18h18', 2)]);
      case 'left': return S([p('m15 18-6-6 6-6', 0)]);
      case 'chev-r': return S([p('m9 18 6-6-6-6', 0)]);
      case 'home': return S([p('M3 9l9-7 9 7v11a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V9z', 0), p('M9 22V12h6v10', 1)]);

      case 'wallet': return S([p('M21 12V7a2 2 0 0 0-2-2H5a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v10a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h14a2 2 0 0 0 2-2v-5z', 0), p('M16 12a1 1 0 1 0 0 2 1 1 0 0 0 0-2z', 1)]);

      case 'image': return S([R('rect', { key: 'r', x: 3, y: 3, width: 18, height: 18, rx: 2 }), c(8.5, 8.5, 1.5, 1), p('M21 15l-5-5L5 21', 2)]);
      case 'copy': return S([R('rect', { key: 'r', x: 9, y: 9, width: 13, height: 13, rx: 2, ry: 2 }), p('M5 15H4a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V4a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h9a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v1', 1)]);

  services() {

  money(n) { return '$' + n.toLocaleString('es-AR'); }

  generateCode() {
    const words = ['FRAS', 'CORTE', 'BIENVE', 'VIP', 'PROMO'];
    const nums = Math.floor(Math.random() * 90 + 10);
    return words[Math.floor(Math.random() * words.length)] + nums;
  }

  toggle(stateKey, field) {
    const cur = this.state[stateKey];
    this.setState({ [stateKey]: { ...cur, [field]: !cur[field] } });
  }

  buildToggle(on, onToggle, color) {
    const R = React.createElement;
    const c = color || this.T().GREEN;
    return R('button', {
      className: 'tog',
      onClick: onToggle,
      style: { width: '44px', height: '26px', borderRadius: '999px', border: 0, background: on ? c : '#2A2A2C', position: 'relative', flex: '0 0 auto' }
    },
      R('span', { style: { position: 'absolute', top: '3px', left: on ? '21px' : '3px', width: '20px', height: '20px', borderRadius: '50%', background: '#fff', transition: 'left .15s' } }));
  }

  buildNav(active) {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T();
    const items = [
      { key: 'home', label: 'Inicio', icon: 'home' },
      { key: 'turnos', label: 'Turnos', icon: 'cal' },
      { key: 'ganancias', label: 'Ganancias', icon: 'wallet' },
      { key: 'settings', label: 'Config.', icon: 'settings', active: true },
    ];
    return R('div', { style: { flex: '0 0 auto', display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-around', padding: '8px 0 18px', borderTop: '1px solid #1E1E20', background: t.BG } },
      items.map(it =>
        R('div', { key: it.key, style: { display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', gap: '3px', cursor: 'pointer', padding: '2px 10px 0' } },
          this.ic(it.icon, 21, it.active ? t.BLUE : t.FAINT),
          R('span', { style: { fontSize: '10px', fontWeight: it.active ? 700 : 500, color: it.active ? t.BLUE : t.FAINT } }, it.label))));
  }

  sectionHeader(icon, title, onBack) {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T();
    return R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '10px', padding: '10px 16px 12px', flex: '0 0 auto', borderBottom: '1px solid #1A1A1C' } },
      onBack ? R('button', { onClick: onBack, style: { width: '32px', height: '32px', borderRadius: '9px', background: t.CARD, border: '1px solid ' + t.BD, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', cursor: 'pointer' } }, this.ic('left', 16, t.MUTED)) : null,
      R('span', { style: { display: 'flex' } }, this.ic(icon, 19, t.BLUE)),
      R('span', { style: { fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '20px', flex: 1 } }, title));
  }

  rowItem(icon, label, value, color) {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T();
    return R('div', { style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '12px', padding: '12px 16px', borderBottom: '1px solid #1A1A1C' } },
      R('span', { style: { width: '34px', height: '34px', borderRadius: '10px', background: t.CARD, border: '1px solid ' + t.BD, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', flex: '0 0 auto' } }, this.ic(icon, 16, color || t.MUTED)),
      R('div', { style: { flex: 1 } },
        R('div', { style: { fontSize: '11px', fontWeight: 700, color: t.FAINT, letterSpacing: '.07em' } }, label.toUpperCase()),
        R('div', { style: { fontSize: '14px', fontWeight: 600, color: t.TEXT, marginTop: '2px' } }, value)));
  }

  // ===================== DRAWER MENU (A) =====================
  menuScreen(variant) {
    const R = React.createElement, t = this.T();
    const items = [
      { icon: 'settings', label: 'Configuración', sub: 'Perfil y negocio', screen: 'config', color: t.BLUE },
      { icon: 'scissors', label: 'Servicios', sub: 'Precios y duración', screen: 'servicios', color: '#B79CFF' },
      { icon: 'box', label: 'Productos', sub: 'Stock y precios', screen: 'productos', color: '#E8A33D' },
      { icon: 'clock', label: 'Horarios', sub: 'Días y disponibilidad', screen: 'horarios', color: '#F26157' },
    ];
    const setScreen = (s) => variant === 'A' ? this.setState({ screenA: s }) : null;
    const curScreen = variant === 'A' ? this.state.screenA : null;

    return R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' } },
      R('div', { style: { padding: '10px 18px 16px', flex: '0 0 auto', borderBottom: '1px solid #1A1A1C' } },
        R('div', { style: { width: '52px', height: '52px', borderRadius: '16px', background: 'linear-gradient(135deg,#2F6BFF,#8B5CF6)', marginBottom: '10px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' } },
          this.ic('scissors', 26, '#fff')),
        R('div', { style: { fontFamily: "'Playfair Display',serif", fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '20px' } }, 'BarberFras'),
        R('div', { style: { fontSize: '12px', color: t.FAINT, marginTop: '2px' } }, 'Panel del peluquero')),
      R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, overflowY: 'auto' } },
        items.map((it, i) =>
          R('div', {
            key: i, className: 'mitem',
            onClick: () => it.screen && setScreen(it.screen),
            style: { display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '12px', padding: '13px 18px', borderBottom: '1px solid #161618', cursor: it.screen ? 'pointer' : 'default', opacity: it.screen ? 1 : 0.5 }
          },
            R('span', { style: { width: '36px', height: '36px', borderRadius: '10px', background: it.color + '15', border: '1px solid ' + it.color + '30', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', flex: '0 0 auto' } },
              this.ic(it.icon, 18, it.color)),
            R('div', { style: { flex: 1 } },
              R('div', { style: { fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '14px' } }, it.label),
              R('div', { style: { fontSize: '11px', color: t.FAINT, marginTop: '1px' } }, it.sub)),
            it.screen ? this.ic('chev-r', 15, t.FAINT) : null))));
  }

  // ===================== CONFIG SCREEN =====================
  configScreen(variant) {

    return R('div', { style: { flex: 1, minHeight: 0, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' } },
      this.sectionHeader('settings', 'Configuración', variant === 'A' ? back : null),

          R('div', { style: { width: '44px', height: '44px', borderRadius: '12px', background: '#2A2A2C', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', margin: '0 auto 8px' } },

          this.rowItem('phone', 'Teléfono', '11 2345 6789', t.GREEN),
          this.rowItem('pin', 'Dirección', 'Av. Corrientes 1234, CABA', t.YELLOW)),
        // divider
        R('div', { style: { margin: '16px 16px 0', padding: '14px', background: t.CARD, border: '1px solid ' + t.BD, borderRadius: '16px' } },

          code
